name:e‚Äçv
info:Deluxe Room
info:Stayed in December 2021
info:Business travelers
info:10 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted December 26, 2021
msg:Nice hotel with rustic wood flooring.  The office desk was massive and built into the wall.  The shelf above the desk had a beautiful vase to add to the relaxing decor.  The tv shelf was a floating shelf which means it's attached to the wall instead of resting on table legs.  This is great because some people can accidentally bump their feet on the TV cabinet.  There was a sitting area with a couch and beautiful glass coffee table by the window looking out on an amazing aerial view of the convention center across the road.  The bed was very comfortable and warm.  The pillows were the perfect softness.  The bathroom had a wonderful tub, separate shower/rain shower, and separate toilet with emergency phone.  The bath mat was a wonderful, soft, fur-like bath mat.  Normally hotels just have a special towel for the floor, so the soft bathmat was awesome!  Will definitely recommend this hotel, and I plan to visit again in the future.
